 1
 Mute Group Chat: This feature is especially important for those who do not want to join a group of friends or relatives where there are many messages

 is saal aae tufaan ko 'phani' (phani Cyclone) naam diya gaya he
 At the same time, in 2018, the storm from the Bay of Bengal was named 'titli'
 yah 'titali' naam pakistan ne diya tha
 Know here how this storm got the name 'fani Cyclone'
 in sabhi aath deshon ne world metrological organijeshan (world Meteorological Organization) ko tufaanon ke naam kii list di hui he
 In this, India gave names like 'agni', 'lightning', 'megh', 'sagar' and 'akash'
 vahiin, pakistan ne 'nilophar', 'bulbul' or 'titali' jaise naam die
 It is from these names that the World Metrological Organization names the storm
 in aath deshon main agar chakravaat aata he to bheje gaye naamon main baari-baari ek naam chunaa jaataa he
 One name is not used again in India for 10 years
 saath hi zyada tabaahi machaane vaale chakravaaton ke naam ko nirast kar diya jaataa he
 This time the storm has been named 'phani' at the suggestion of Bangladesh
 vahiin, america har saal tufaanon ke 21 naamon kii suchi taiyaar karata he
 However, every alphabet in English is named
 lekin Q,U,X,Y or z alfabet se tufaan kaa naam rakhane kii parampara nahin he
 If more than 21 storms come in a year, then they are named after the Greek alphabet alpha, beta, gamma
 in naamon main od-evan kaa formula apanaaya jaataa he
 For example, in years, a cyclone is named after women, while the storms in even years are based on men
 kehane kaa matlab he ki od saal jaise ki 2019, 2021 or 2023 main aane vaale tufaanon ke naam auraton ke naam par rakhe jaaenge
 At the same time, the names of storms in the year such as 2018, 2020 and 2022 will be based on the names of men
